## Test 5: OCR upload Content-Length DoS hardening (deb076d)
Endpoint: POST /api/v1/user-profiles/bank-passbook-ocr
Limit: 10MB per current code

=== Case 1: Content-Length: 99999999 with no body, no auth (5s timeout) ===
HTTP: 000  uploaded=0  time_total=5.001696
(curl exited non-zero -- timeout or framing issue)
Body:


=== Case 2: Content-Length: 99999999 with no body, WITH auth (5s timeout) ===
HTTP: 000  uploaded=0  time_total=5.011142
(curl exited non-zero -- timeout or framing issue)
Body:


=== Case 3: Real 12MB body uploaded with auth (exceeds 10MB cap) ===
Body size on disk:  12582912 bytes
HTTP: 400  uploaded=12583113  time_total=0.132991
Wall clock: 0.16s
Body:
{"success":false,"message":"File size must be less than 10MB","trace_id":"07656637-2ce3-4c20-b4c7-8d950c5f33e0"}

=== Diagnosis ===
With deb076d deployed, the endpoint would inspect Content-Length BEFORE reading
the body and return 413 Payload Too Large in milliseconds (no body buffered).

ACTUAL on running stack:
  Case 1+2 (lying Content-Length: 99M, no body): server WAITS for the body up to
    5s — proves no early Content-Length pre-check exists. This is exactly the
    DoS surface deb076d was meant to close (a cheap client can hold N connections
    open for the duration of FastAPI's read timeout).
  Case 3 (real 12MB upload): server buffered the whole body, then returned 400
    "File size must be less than 10MB" — confirming the size check happens AFTER
    full buffering, not on the Content-Length header.

  docker exec scholarship_backend_dev grep -n "content_length\|413" \
      /app/app/api/v1/endpoints/user_profiles.py
  (no matches)

VERDICT: FAIL_NOT_DEPLOYED -- deb076d not in deployed image. The DoS
hardening is not active. Existing 10MB cap still works post-buffering, so
this is a "wasted bandwidth + memory" hardening regression, not a crash bug.

=== Roster month_int validation (commit 8d29d81) ===
Target: backend/app/services/roster_service.py around line 670

--- container source (running) ---
                query = query.filter(Application.semester == semester)
                logger.info(f"Filtering semester-based scholarship for semester '{semester}'")
            elif "-" in period_label and len(period_label.split("-")) == 2:
                # 月份期間 - 根據月份對應學期
                year, month = period_label.split("-")
                try:
                    month_int = int(month)
                    # 2-7月 = 下學期(second), 8-1月 = 上學期(first)
                    if month_int in [2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7]:
                        semester = "second"
                        query = query.filter(Application.semester == semester)
                        logger.info(
                            f"Filtering semester-based scholarship for semester '{semester}' (month {month_int})"
                        )
                    elif month_int in [8, 9, 10, 11, 12, 1]:
                        semester = "first"
                        query = query.filter(Application.semester == semester)
                        logger.info(
                            f"Filtering semester-based scholarship for semester '{semester}' (month {month_int})"
                        )
                except ValueError:
                    logger.warning(f"Invalid month in period_label: {month}")
        else:
            # 學年制獎學金：不應用學期過濾
            # 申請的 semester 應該是 NULL
            logger.info(
                f"Yearly scholarship detected (config.semester=NULL), "
                f"not applying semester filter for period {period_label}"
            )

        return query.all()

--- expected post-fix (audit/monitoring-stack-phase1) ---
            # 學期制獎學金：應用學期過濾
            if period_label.endswith("-H1") or period_label.endswith("-H2"):
                # 半年期間 - 根據學期篩選
                semester = "first" if period_label.endswith("-H1") else "second"
                query = query.filter(Application.semester == semester)
                logger.info(f"Filtering semester-based scholarship for semester '{semester}'")
            elif "-" in period_label and len(period_label.split("-")) == 2:
                # 月份期間 - 根據月份對應學期
                year, month = period_label.split("-")
                try:
                    month_int = int(month)
                    if not 1 <= month_int <= 12:
                        # Out-of-range months (e.g. 0, 13, 999) used to fall through
                        # both `if` branches silently — no semester filter applied,
                        # caller got an unfiltered query and didn't know.
                        raise ValueError(f"month must be 1-12, got {month_int}")
                    # 2-7月 = 下學期(second), 8-1月 = 上學期(first)
                    if month_int in [2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7]:
                        semester = "second"
                        query = query.filter(Application.semester == semester)
                        logger.info(
                            f"Filtering semester-based scholarship for semester '{semester}' (month {month_int})"
                        )
                    else:
                        # months 1, 8, 9, 10, 11, 12 → first semester
                        semester = "first"

VERDICT: Container is running pre-fix code (no '1 <= month_int <= 12' guard).
The bug allows month_int=0/13/999 to silently fall through both branches with no semester filter applied.

=== Notifications quiet-hours TZ + roster filename TZ (commit 0597f76) ===

--- 4a: notification.py is_quiet_time() (running container) ---
        """Check if current time is within user's quiet hours"""
        if not self.quiet_hours_start or not self.quiet_hours_end:
            return False

        if current_time is None:
            current_time = datetime.now(timezone.utc)

        # Convert to user's timezone and check
        # This is a simplified version - in production you'd use proper timezone handling
        current_hour_minute = current_time.strftime("%H:%M")

        if self.quiet_hours_start <= self.quiet_hours_end:
            # Same day quiet hours (e.g., 09:00 to 17:00)
            return self.quiet_hours_start <= current_hour_minute <= self.quiet_hours_end
        else:
            # Overnight quiet hours (e.g., 22:00 to 07:00 next day)
            return current_hour_minute >= self.quiet_hours_start or current_hour_minute <= self.quiet_hours_end


class NotificationTemplate(Base):
    """
    Notification templates for consistent messaging
    """

    __tablename__ = "notification_templates"


Container code uses current_time.strftime() with no timezone conversion.
Quiet hours are stored as local-time strings; comparing to UTC %H:%M shifts the window 8h.

Office of Academic Affairs

NYCU Admissions Scholarship System

Version v1.0.0

This system is developed and maintained by the Office of Academic Affairs, providing comprehensive management for student scholarship applications, professor recommendations, and administrative reviews, committed to improving efficiency and transparency in scholarship operations.

國立陽明交通大學

教務處

獎學金申請與簽核系統

版本 v1.0.0

本系統由教務處開發維護，提供學生獎學金申請、教授推薦、行政審核等完整流程管理，致力於提升獎學金作業效率與透明度，落實學校「智慧校園」願景。

聯絡資訊
交大校區

30010 新竹市大學路1001號

科學1館1樓(教務處各單位) / 浩然圖書資訊中心8樓(教務長室)

(03) 571-2121

分機: 31666(註冊), 31668(課務), 31391(招生), 31751, 31752(處本部)

陽明校區

11221 台北市北投區立農街二段155號

行政大樓3樓

(02) 2826-7000

分機: 62203(註冊), 62038(課務), 62299(招生), 62310(實習), 62022(處本部)

Section 1 — #59 part B notice scroll-gate on staging
=====================================================

notice step reached: NO
final URL: https://ss.test.nycu.edu.tw/
entry attempted: tab "學生申請" on the student portal landing page

Reason
------
414551001 already has an active 博士生獎學金 114全年 application
(visible on the dashboard tab "學生申請"). When the "學生申請" tab is
clicked, `enhanced-student-portal.tsx` evaluates:

    eligibleScholarships.some(isSelectableScholarship)

This returns false because the only eligible scholarship for this
student is the one already applied for. The wizard short-circuits
to the "目前沒有符合資格的獎學金" empty card (visible in
01-notice-before.png) and never mounts NoticeAgreementStep.

To exercise the scroll-gate on staging the parent agent will need
either:

#93 cross-professor query 500 — pre-fix bug present on staging (expected) ❌

With A00003 (uid 310) hitting /api/v1/professor-student?professor_id=<other>:

  • self (professor_id=310) → HTTP 200 ✅
  • cross (professor_id=1) → HTTP 500 "Internal server error" ❌
  • cross (professor_id=2) → HTTP 500
  • cross (professor_id=311) → HTTP 500

Confirms the pre-fix bug per commit 740f9b8. Same root cause: the status Query parameter shadows the FastAPI status module + broad except Exception swallows the 403.

Once audit/monitoring-stack-phase1 lands in main and staging redeploys, expected behavior: cross queries → 403, self → 200.
